  • @AmplifyUkraine #325727 04:59 PM, 02 Jan 2023
    TRANSLATION :
    During the winter, PCU activists in the Volyn region force a priest to leave the parish house.

    This happened on the last day of 2022 in the village of Kremenets. Earlier, they took away the church from the priest and forced him to write a receipt for eviction from the parish house.

    These actions of the activists and the police are illegal, because according to the law, it is the religious community, not the territorial one, that is responsible for this. We should note that in early summer in the village of Kremenets there was a meeting of the territorial community, at which an illegal decision was made to transfer the local St. Nicholas Church to the jurisdiction of the "WTO".

    The priest served in the church for more than 30 years and built the parish house at his own expense.

    We should add that such actions are already prerequisites for a religious war in the country.

    TRANSLATION :
    üöô The Ministry of Internal Affairs presented new rules for obtaining a driver's license

    Ukraine plans to introduce significant changes in driving schools for obtaining a driver's license, the Main Service Center of the Ministry of Internal Affairs announced. The latest technologies will be introduced into the exam process to make them as transparent, accessible and efficient as possible.

    What are they planning to introduce?

    Verification and access to the exam class is planned - a person who passes the theoretical exam will enter the exam class, where there will be a camera at the entrance. It will recognize the face of the driver candidate, which will allow the person to be directed to a randomly determined workplace in the Unified State Register of the Ministry of Internal Affairs to pass the theoretical exam.

    üëâ The theory exam will be held in the examination classroom under the following conditions:
    - FACE ID identification of the person during the entire examination process;
    - fixation of the face and screen in case of a negative answer to the exam question;
    - prevention of remote access to workplaces;
    - control over the behavior of the person;
    - video recording of the exam process.

    üëâ cars in the service centers of the Ministry of Internal Affairs will be equipped with a video recorder with 4 cameras - front, rear, two interior projections, an internal monitor to control the angle and operation of the video recorder, alarm sensors and duplicate pedals.

    üëâ purchase of vehicles with built-in technical equipment of various categories for the service centers of the Ministry of Internal Affairs. That is, now future drivers do not need to look for trucks, cars with trailers, motorcycles for rent, if they are not in the service center of the Ministry of Internal Affairs. Now all these vehicles will be there, and everyone will be able to pass a practical exam.

    üìπ In addition, it is planned to bring video web cameras located on workstations in the classroom to the examiner's workplace, which will allow you to control the entire process online.

  • @AmplifyUkraine #325784 05:58 PM, 02 Jan 2023
    TRANSLATION :
    ‚ùóÔ∏èNew money: what banknotes began to be withdrawn from circulation on January 1

    National Bank from January 1, 2023 gradually began to withdraw from circulation paper banknotes of 5, 10, 20 and 100 hryvnia samples 2003-2007. They will be replaced by coins of 5 and 10 hryvnia and a new generation of 20 and 100 hryvnia banknotes, the press service of the NBU.

    Ukrainian banks will not issue such banknotes from cash offices for all types of cash transactions.
    NBU will stop backing such banknotes to the cash registers of banks.
    As a consequence, once in the banks, the previous generation banknotes will no longer be returned to circulation, but will be withdrawn from circulation and transferred to the NBU for further disposal.

    üó£"But such banknotes remain valid means of payment. Citizens will be able to continue to pay with them without restrictions, they do not need to be specifically exchanged," the statement said.

    In occupied Crimea "police" visited activists: warned about inadmissibility of violation of Russian legislation

    Several people in different districts of the temporarily occupied by Russia Crimea reported to the public initiative "Crimean Solidarity" on New Year's Eve that they were visited by the illegal "police" and warned about the inadmissibility of violating the law.

    The security forces came to Ebazer Islamov and Eskender Dzhelialov in Nizhnegorsk district, to Elmaz Akimova in Simferopol district and to Seytosman Karaliev in Sudak.

    The document from the "police" was issued as an "official warning". It says that the occupiers held preventive talks with the activists to prevent violations of Russian legislation and the possibility of bringing them to justice.

    In particular, the "police" referred to Article 19.3 of the Administrative Code of the Russian Federation on disobedience to a police officer.

    Two residents of Kryvoozerska territorial community of Mykolaiv region will be brought to court for draft evasion

    According to the investigation, the accused, being liable for military service, received a summons to be sent to the military unit through authorized persons at their place of residence.

    However, realizing the illegality of their actions, the men refused to be called up for mobilization, thus evading military service.

    The men face imprisonment for a term of 3 to 5 years.

    TRANSLATION :
    SBU announces first suspicions for shelling of civilian objects in Ukraine: evidence on Russian general and Russian Navy admiral collected

    SBU investigators collected high-quality evidence base on two representatives of the Russian high command, who are responsible for shelling of civilian objects in Ukraine.

    One of them is the Commander of the Long-Range Aviation of the Russian Aerospace Forces, Colonel-General Serhii Kobylash. And the other is the former Commander of the Black Sea Fleet of the Russian Federation Admiral Igor Osipov.

    Both of them were notified of suspicion under two articles of the Criminal Code of Ukraine:

    ‚ñ™Ô∏è Part 2 of Art. 437 (planning, preparation, outbreak and conduct of aggressive war);
    ‚ñ™Ô∏è—á. 3 Art. 110 (encroachment on the territorial integrity and inviolability of Ukraine).

    These are the first suspicions that Ukraine announces specifically for the shelling of civilian objects in Ukraine.

    The maximum sanction of the articles provides for punishment in the form of life imprisonment.

    Thus, during the investigation, the SBU investigators found that since the beginning of the full-scale invasion, Serhiy Kobylash has been following the instructions of the highest military and political leadership of Russia to destroy Ukrainian cities.

    It is on his orders that Russian invaders carry out massive missile attacks on residential buildings, hospitals and critical infrastructure in different regions of Ukraine.

    To carry out air attacks, the enemy uses strategic missile carriers Tu-160, Tu-95MS, as well as long-range missile carriers-bombers Tu-22M3, armed with cruise missiles of the types X-555, X-101, X-55 and X-22.

    As for Igor Osipov, according to the investigation, in the period from February 24 to August 10, 2022, the official gave orders to conduct systematic missile strikes from the Black Sea on Ukrainian densely populated areas.

    Enemy attacks were carried out with high-precision guided cruise missiles "3M14-Kalibr" from Russian warships.

    The pre-trial investigation is ongoing.

    üè† How can internally displaced persons apply for a housing subsidy?

    IDPs can apply for a subsidy for housing and communal services at the place of actual residence, the Ministry of Reintegration reports. In this case, the conclusion of a lease agreement is not required, and the composition of the household is indicated by the applicant in the declaration.

    üìçIn order to receive a subsidy, IDPs need to apply personally to one of these bodies:
    ‚ûû authorized official of the executive body of the village, settlement, city council of the relevant territorial community;
    ‚ûû administrative service center;
    ‚ûû service center of the Pension Fund of Ukraine.

    üì≤ You can also apply for the subsidy in electronic form on one of the services:
    ‚ûû portal "Diia";
    ‚ûû web portal of electronic services of the PFU;
    ‚ûû mobile application of the Pension Fund of Ukraine (available for download on Android and IOS).

    ü™™ What documents are required to receive a subsidy?
    ‚úîÔ∏è Application for a subsidy (in the prescribed form);
    ‚úîÔ∏è Declaration of income and expenses (in the prescribed form);
    ‚úîÔ∏è Data on household members;
    ‚úîÔ∏è Passport, taxpayer registration number (RNOKPP);
    ‚úîÔ∏è Certificate of IDP status.

    The amount of assistance depends on the cost of housing and communal services used by the family and its income level. At the same time, the housing allowance provided to IDPs is not taken into account in the total income when assigning a housing subsidy.

    üëâ You can find out whether you have been granted a subsidy and its amount online at the link. Information in the register is searched by household address. After filling in the necessary data, all information on the status of the application for a subsidy will appear.

    Operational situation in the region as of the morning of January 3.

    At night, Russians struck both the frontline and the relative rear.

    Druzhkivka, located far from the frontline, suffered three strikes: the Ice Arena was destroyed, the buildings of the Academy of Sciences, the bus station, a church, a residential building and outbuildings were damaged.     In the Horlivka sector, 1 person died in Bakhmut. A house was damaged in Ivanivske. In Blahodatne of Soledar community 2 houses were damaged.

  • @AmplifyUkraine #326184 09:12 AM, 03 Jan 2023
    TRANSLATION :
    ‚è≥9:00 Minute of silence

    üïØ Military pilot Roman Pasulka died on February 24, 2022 in an air battle with Russian occupiers, defending Kyiv region. He was 22 years old.

    Roman was born in the village of Raukhivka, Odesa region. In childhood, he moved with his family to Chernihiv region. He studied at Nizhyn school ‚Ññ17. Subsequently, he chose the military path. In 2021, he graduated from the Kharkiv National Air Force University named after Ivan Kozhedub, where he received the qualification of a 3rd class pilot.

    After graduation, he served in the 40th Tactical Aviation Brigade of the Air Force of the Armed Forces of Ukraine, which is located in Vasylkiv, Kyiv region. He flew on MiG-29 fighter aircraft.

    On the first day of the full-scale war, Roman defended the Ukrainian sky. He held back the attack of the Russian military, covering his colleagues and protecting civilians.

    "On February 24, when Russian troops shamefully invaded the territory of Ukraine, Roman received a combat mission and without hesitation took to the skies to defend his homeland. Saving thousands of civilian lives - at the cost of his own life. In the memory of colleagues, Roman will forever remain sincere, smiling, full of many plans for life, which, unfortunately, were not destined to come true. His parents brought Roman up to be a real warrior, strong-willed and courageous patriot of his homeland... Roman was a good student, despite his young age - a professionally trained pilot," - the brigade informed.

    Senior Lieutenant Pasulka was posthumously awarded the Order "For Courage" of the III degree. The officer was buried in Nizhyn, Chernihiv region. Roman is survived by his parents, sister and beloved girlfriend.

    TRANSLATION :
    On January 18-19, NATO military leaders will meet. Ukraine is among the main topics

    The Military Committee - NATO's highest military body - will meet on 18-19 January 2023 in Brussels.

    This is reported by the NATO press service.

    Admiral Rob Bauer, Chairman of the Military Committee, will chair the meeting, which will be attended by the Chiefs of Defence of the Alliance and their counterparts from invited Finland and Sweden.

    The Military Committee meeting will allow the 32 Chiefs of Defence to meet and discuss issues of strategic importance to the Alliance.

    NATO Secretary General Jens Stoltenberg will join the Military Committee at the opening session to present the latest political objectives and discuss the security challenges facing the Alliance.

    One of the panels of the Military Committee will be dedicated to NATO's continued support to Ukraine.

    "According to the military intelligence of Ukraine, the Russians will try to continue offensive actions next year. They failed to achieve their goal in any of the directions.
